<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ширинка.html>шири́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">širínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ширинка.html>шири́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ширинка.html>шири́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ширинка.html>шири́нок</a></b>)

***широкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кий</a> (557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*širokъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">širókij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ши́ре</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:широчайший.html>широча́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wide, broad
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проход.html>прохо́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>širókij</b> proxód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wide passage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>broad, extensive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кругозор.html>кругозо́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>širókij</b> krugozór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">broad outlook; wide range of interests</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́ких</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгля́дов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čelovék <b>širókix</b> vzgljádov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">open-minded person</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:намерение.html>наме́рения</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>širókije</b> namérenija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">grandiose intentions</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ры</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кого</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:потребление.html>потребле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">továry <b>širókovo</b> potreblénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">consumer goods</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:публика.html>пу́блика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>širókaja</b> públika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the general public</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">short form only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> too loose, too wide, loose-fitting <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of clothing and shoes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:штаны.html>штаны́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широки́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne éti štaný <b>širokí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">these trousers are too loose for me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>generous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>širókaja</b> dušá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">generous spirit</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ширше</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">širše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is a common but proscribed superlative form.</li></ul>

***шить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a> (7123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šiti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*sjū́ˀtei</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*syuh₁-</i>.
Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">siūti</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sew</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">suō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сшить.html>сшить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sew
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šitʹ</b> na mašínke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sew on a machine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> only  imperfective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be occupied with sewing, to tailor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>Чем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заниматься.html>занима́ется</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Она</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шьёт</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Čem oná zanimájetsja? Ona <b>šʹjót</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What is she? She’s a dressmaker.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to order (e.g., a dress)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сшить.html>сшить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:костюм.html>костю́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> Левинсона</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xočú sšitʹ sebé kostjúm u Levinsona</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I want to order a suit from Levinson’s</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">only  imperfective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to embroider
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лотом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šitʹ</b> zólotom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">embroider in gold</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шитый.html>ши́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лыми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́тками</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šito bélymi nítkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blatantly obvious, transparent to anyone</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">embroidered in white thread</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šitʹ</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cook up charges</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to embroider the case</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лыко.html>лы́ком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шитый.html>шит</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">(on) ne lýkom šit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(he) was not born yesterday</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">(he) was not embroidered in bast</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to nail planking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плот.html>плот</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šitʹ</b> plot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a raft</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***шиш.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>шиш</a> (12159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>шиш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šiš</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шиш.html>шиша́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шиш.html>шиши́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шиш.html>шише́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rude gesture in which the hand makes a fist and the thumb is stuck between the index and middle fingers, which indicates "nothing for you, nuts to you"</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not the same vulgar meaning that this gesture has in Western European countries such as Germany.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фига.html>фи́га</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">fíga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуля.html>ду́ля</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dúlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кукиш.html>ку́киш</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kúkiš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***шишка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шишка.html>шишка</a> (6595)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">шишька</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šišĭka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šišьka</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шишка.html>ши́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šíška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шишка.html>ши́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шишка.html>ши́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шишка.html>ши́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cone, strobilus (fruit of conifers)</li>
<li>bump, bunion</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> masculine or feminine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boss</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>ши́ш</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>

Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:важный.html>ва́жный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>» — <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> согласовываться <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:важный.html>ва́жный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:шишка.html>ши́шку</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:шишка.html>ши́шек</a></i>).
</p><p>Непроизводное.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-шишк-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:нечто.html>нечто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступающий.html>выступа́ющее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:округлый.html>окру́глой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a></i>.

Зализняка).

***шкатулка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкатулка.html>шкату́лка</a> (11278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szkatułka</i> (diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szkatuła</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">scatola</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">castula</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Casket_ivory_Louvre_UCAD4417.jpg/220px-Casket_ivory_Louvre_UCAD4417.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="163" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Casket_ivory_Louvre_UCAD4417.jpg/330px-Casket_ivory_Louvre_UCAD4417.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Casket_ivory_Louvre_UCAD4417.jpg/440px-Casket_ivory_Louvre_UCAD4417.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1850" data-file-height="1370" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:шкатулка.html>шкату́лка</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкатулка.html>шкату́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">škatúlka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкатулка.html>шкату́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкатулка.html>шкату́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкатулка.html>шкату́лок</a></b>)
</p>

***шкаф.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкаф.html>шкаф</a> (1742)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">schap</i> and/or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scap</i> (both “cupboard, cabinet, coffer”). The word-final <i>-ф</i> might be due to inference by the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> cognate <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schaf</i>, which usually meant “barrel, keg”, however. Possibly it is merely a phonetic irregularity.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкаф.html>шкаф</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">škaf</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкаф.html>шка́фа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкаф.html>шкафы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкаф.html>шкафо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cupboard</li>
<li>wardrobe, closet</li>
<li>locker, cabinet</li>
<li>bookcase, shelves</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шкафно́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">škafnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шка́фный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">škáfnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкафчик.html>шка́фчик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">škáfčik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкафчик.html>шка́фчик</a> (12925)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шквал.html>шквал</a> (17382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1765. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">squall</i>, from Scandinavian language (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">skval</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">skvala</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***школа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́ла</a> (382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szkoła</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">school</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">schola</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σχολή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skholḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́ла</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">škóla</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́лы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>school
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">музика́лная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́ла</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">muzikálnaja <b>škóla</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">music school</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>schoolhouse</li>
<li>academy</li>
<li>university</li></ol>

***шкура.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкура.html>шку́ра</a> (2552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">skóra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skora</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bast, skin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)ker-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">carnage</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cortex</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">carrion</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">corium</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scurf</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">excoriate</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скорый.html>скора́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skorá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of animals</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> skin, pelt, coat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bastard, scum</li>
